STAT table

STAT table

Info

Sabon Next LT Regular (sabonnreglt_57607.ttf)

STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

No check of STAT table for static fonts included, yet. Static fonts do not need to have a STAT table. It is only recommended by Microsoft, not required.
More infos here:
https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/typography/opentype/spec/stat

Info

Sabon Next LT Italic (sabonnregitalt_57602.ttf)

STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

No check of STAT table for static fonts included, yet. Static fonts do not need to have a STAT table. It is only recommended by Microsoft, not required.
More infos here:
https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/typography/opentype/spec/stat

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'SabonNextLT-Italic', Everything looks good.

Sabon Next LT Italic (sabonnregitalt_57602.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'SabonNextLT-Italic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Please verify against job spec.

You may use this font as permitted by the EULA for the product in which this font is included to display and print content. You may only (i) embed this font in content as permitted by the embedding restrictions included in this font; and (ii) temporarily download this font to a printer or other output device to help print content. This web font file is intended for use with the Microsoft Sway application only, and not for further use or distribution of any kind.
but should be:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

Sabon Next LT Bold (sabonnbollt_57570.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'SabonNextLT-Bold', Everything looks good.

Pass

kern

Warning

Sabon Next LT Regular (sabonnreglt_57607.ttf)

kern

-/-

Check if 'kern' table in TTF font.

Font has 'kern' table. Please verify if font requires kern table or if only GPOS kerning should be in font.
For example: PowerPoint only supports a flat GPOS kerning or a kern table. So, if the customer requires PowerPoint support, a kern table is necessary.
